Padmagupta alias Parimala
Navasāhasāṅkacarita 
prathamaḥ sargaḥ
avyāt sa vo yasya nisargavakraḥ spṛśaty adhijyasmaracāpalīlām 
jaṭāpinaddhoragarājaratna marīcilīḍhobhayakoṭir induḥ  PNc 
jaṭāhiratnadyutipāṭalo 'vyāt sa vaḥ śaśī śaṅkaramauliratnam 
śrutāv aśokāṅkurakautukena yaṃ kartum icchaty acalendrakanyā  PNc 
kumbhasthalī rakṣatu vo vikīrṇa sindūrareṇur dviradānanasya 
praśāntaye vighnatamaśchaṭānāṃ niṣṭhyūtabālātapapallaveva  PNc 
cakṣus tad unmeṣi sadā mukhe vaḥ sārasvataṃ śāśvatam āvir astu 
paśyanti yenāvahitāḥ kavīndrās triviṣṭapābhyantaravarti vastu  PNc 
prācīnakavivarṇanam
tattvaspṛśas te kavayaḥ purāṇāḥ śrībhartṛmeṇṭhapramukhā jayanti 
nistṛṃśadhārāsadṛśena yeṣāṃ vaidarbhamārgeṇa giraḥ pravṛttāḥ  PNc 
pūrṇendubimbād api sundarāṇi teṣām adūre purato yaśāṃsi 
ye bhartṛmeṇṭhādikavīndrasūkti vyaktopadiṣṭena pathā prayānti  PNc 
sarasvatīkalpalataikakandaṃ vandāmahe vākpatirājadevam 
yasya prasādād vayam apy ananya kavīndracīrṇe pathi sañcarāmaḥ  PNc 
divaṃ yiyāsur mama vāci mudrām adatta yāṃ vākpatirājadevaḥ 
tasyānujanmā kavibāndhavasya bhinatti tāṃ saṃprati sindhurājaḥ  PNc 
kaveḥ śālīnatādi
naite kavīndrāḥ kati kāvyabandhe tad eṣa rājñā kim ahaṃ niyuktaḥ 
kiṃ vālukāparvatake dhareyam āropyate satsu kulācaleṣu  PNc 
aho mahatsāhasam etad eva yad varṇaṇīyo navasāhasāṅkaḥ 
dūre paricchedakathā hi satyam etadguṇānām udadher apāṃ ca  PNc 
bhaktyāthavāsyaiva mama prabandhe sūkṣmo 'yam unmīlati śaktileśaḥ 
ullaṅghito yat kapinā payodhiḥ sevānubhavaḥ sa raghūdvahasya  PNc 
samatsare cetasi durjanānāṃ na jātucit sūktiguṇo guṇāya 
nisargakṛṣṇendravadhūkapole nirarthakaḥ kuṅkumapattrabhaṅgaḥ  PNc 
kim anyad asyāś caritair nṛpasya muktāvadātaiḥ kṛtamaṇḍanāyāḥ 
madīyasūkter mukulībhavantu svabhāvaśuddhāni satāṃ manāṃsi  PNc 
namo 'stu sāhityarasāya tasmai niṣiktam antaḥ pṛṣatāpi yasya 
suvarṇatāṃ vaktram upaiti sadhor durvarṇatāṃ yāti ca durjanasya  PNc 
śrīsāhasāṅkojjvalakīrtigarbhā mamāthavā kaṃ na haranti vācaḥ 
kasyātra lobhāya na śuktayas tā muktā hi yāsām udare sphuranti  PNc 
pratijñā
etāny avantīśvarapārijāta jātāni tārāpatipāṇḍurāṇi 
sampraty ahaṃ paśyata
digvadhūnāṃ yaśaḥprasūnāny avataṃsayāmi  PNc 
atha ujjayinīvarṇanam
asti kṣitaūjjayinīti nāmnā purī vihāyasy amarāvatīva 
babandha yasyāṃ padam indrakalpaḥ śrīvikramāditya iti kṣitīśaḥ  PNc 
āmañjuguñjatkalahaṃsapaṅkti vikasvarāmbhojarajaḥpiśaṅgā 
ābhāti yasyāḥ parikhā nitambe saśabdajambūnadamekhaleva  PNc 
prākāravapracchalataḥ śarīram āvartya līlāśayanaṃ murāreḥ 
yatrāntarasthāyinidhānarakṣāṃ vidhātum unmagna ivoragendraḥ  PNc 
pade pade sāndrasudhojjvalāni gṛhāṇi yā nākasadāṃ bibharti 
abhyudgatānīva phaṇīndralokam āpūrya tadbhūmibhṛtāṃ yaśāṃsi  PNc 
himacchaṭāhāribhir aṃśujālaiḥ prālambimuktāphalajālakāni 
vilāsinīvibhramamandirāṇi yasyāṃ hasantīva parasparasya  PNc 
gṛhāṇi yasyāṃ savarāṅganāni varāṅganā rūpapuraskṛtāṅgyaḥ 
rūpaṃ samunmīlitasadvilāsam astraṃ vilāsāḥ kusumāyudhasya  PNc

avāpya yasyāṃ gṛhadīrghikāccha vaiḍūryasopānamayūkhasakhyam

kim ayaṃ mayi saṃbhramo 'yam āstāṃ kim ayaṃ na eva janaḥ paricchadas te 
upacāraviśeṣasaṃvidhāne pratipaccandra iva uditas tvam eva  PNc 
bhavadiṅgitavedinaiva pṛṣṭā yad anenāham upāntavartinā te 
kim u tat kathayāmi sammataṃ cet kriyatāṃ me svayam ājñayā prasādaḥ  PNc 
nāyakanideśaḥ
abhidhehi lavaḥ kutūhalasya tvadudantaśravaṇe mamāpi jātaḥ 
iti sā vasudhāpater nideśād atha pātālavilāsinī jagāda  PNc 
bhujaṅgalokavarṇanam
sa tava śrutim āpta eva tāvat smaralīlābhavanaṃ bhujaṅgalokaḥ 
upayāti yad ekadeśasāmyaṃ na mahī nāpi purī purandarasya  PNc 
atidurlabhasūryabhāsi yasmiṃs tamasām ullasatāṃ tiraskriyāyai 
phaṇino 'ruṇakāntibhiḥ śirasthair maṇibhir bālam ivātapaṃ vahanti  PNc 
anulimpati rodasī yathenduḥ prabhayā māṃ na tathety asūyayeva 
paṭu yaḥ pramādāvilāsahāsa stabakair induparamparāḥ prasūte  PNc 
savilāsam udastahastamuktair nikarair digdviradendraśīkarāṇām 
parito nicitāḥ sadaiva yasmin kakubhas tārikā ivāvabhānti  PNc 
pratibhāti dadhan phaṇākalāpe pṛthivīṃ yatra saḥ śeṣanāgarājaḥ 
nabhaso nipatañ javena bhittvā jagatīṃ gāṅga iva cyutaḥ pravāhaḥ  PNc 
bhogavatīvarṇanam
viditā khalu vāsukes trilokyāṃ harakaṇṭhābharaṇasya bhogibhartuḥ 
lalitādbhutabhūmir asti tasmin nagarī bhogavatīti rājadhānī  PNc 
maṇiharmyatalāni ratnadīpāḥ phaṇikāntārdhavilokitāni vīṇāḥ 
ṛtavo 'py akhilāḥ sametya yatra smarasāmrājyamahādhuraṃ vahanti  PNc 
anupādhir upāhṛto vikāsaḥ kamalair yatra vilāsadīrghikāsu 
api yatra kumudvatībhir astaḥ sahajaś candramarīcipakṣapātaḥ  PNc 
abhikān abhisartum udyataḥ san sapadi vyālavilāsinīsamūhaḥ 
bhavati svaphaṇāmaṇipradīpe timirotsāriṇi yatra sābhyasūyaḥ  PNc 
adhirohati yatra vaṃśamuktā paṭalasmerataṭā surasravantī 
saritaḥ śriyam īrṣyayeva tasyāḥ suvate mauktikam eva yat payāṃsi  PNc 
atikāntaguṇābhirāmamūrtir madhureṇa dhvaninā manoharantī 
vidadhāti sadaiva yatra yūnāṃ padam aṅke vanitā ca vallakī ca  PNc 
śataśo vilasanty udaṃśuratna stabakāḥ kalpalatā yad aṅgaṇeṣu 
pratimandriram evam eva yasyām api cintāmaṇayaḥ pade luṭhanti  PNc 
api dattakutūhalāḥ surāṇām api vāñcchāpadam ekapiṅgalasya 
api nirviṣayā manorathānām uragān yatra vibhūtayaḥ śrayante  PNc 
vasati svayam eva yatra devaḥ sadā kalpitahāṭakeśvarākhyaḥ 
smaram ūrdhvavilocanārciṣīva tripuraṃ yaḥ śarapāvake juhāva  PNc

śaṅkhapālavarṇanam
nijavaṃśaviśeṣako 'sti tasyām uragāṇām adhipaḥ saḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ 
srag asāv iti yat phaṇāsu dhatte vasudhāṃ vāsukinā samānasāraḥ  PNc 
śaśiprabhāvarṇanam
jagadekalalāma tasya kanyā guṇavaty asti śaśiprabhā nāmnā 
sahasaiva phaṇabhṛtāṃ praviṣṭā bhuvane rāhubhayād ivendulekhā  PNc 
na kayāpy atiśayyate 'tiśīghraṃ yad iyaṃ kandukakeliṣu bhramantī 
aparaṃ kṛtam arthavat tad asyāḥ sutarāṃ nāma sakhībhir āśugeti  PNc 
sphuradadbhutarūpasampadāṃ tām anukartuṃ kalayāpi dhārṣṭyam eti 
na ratir na śacī na citralekhā na ghṛtācī na tilottamā na rambhā  PNc 
surakinnarasiddhakanyakābhiḥ svakalābhyāsavatībhir āptasakhyā 
nikhilāsu gatā paraṃ prakarṣaṃ śitadhīḥ śaiśavas eva yā kalāsu  PNc 
anivāritakelikautukā sā sutanuḥ snehavaṃśavadena pitrā 
viharaty apacīyamānabālyā haraśaile malaye himālaye ca  PNc 
adhunā puno 'tra vindhyapade viharantyāḥ kusumāvacūḍanāmni 
kvacid apy agamat palāyya tasyāś capalaḥ kelimṛgo mṛgāyatākṣyāḥ  PNc 
ativatsalayā samaṃ sakhībhir vipine taṃ paritas tayā vicitya 
puline saritaḥ śaśāṅkasūteḥ śramavatyeyam anīyata triyāmā  PNc 
kalahaṃsakalasvanair vibuddhā parivārapramadānideśitaṃ sā 
nikaṣā niculapravālaśayyāṃ tam atha prekṣitavaty āptanidram  PNc 
tapanīyaśilīmukhas tadaṅge cakitaṃ citrarucau tayā ca dṛṣṭaḥ 
jalade lalitendracāpabhaktau ahimāṃśor iva bhāsuro mayūkhaḥ  PNc 
aravindadalatviṣā kareṇa svayam utpāṭya sakautukaṃ gṛhīte 
avalokitam etayātha tasmin vijayāṅke navasāhasāṅkanāma  PNc 
aviśan naranātha nāma pūrvaṃ hṛdaye 'syāḥ sahasātha puṣpaketuḥ 
amṛtāṃśumarīciluptanidre labhate yat kumude 'ntaraṃ dvirephaḥ  PNc 
navameghamalīmasād yugānte vasudhām uddharato rathāṅgapāṇeḥ 
paritaḥ śramavāribindavo ye nirapīyanta payodhaśuktiyūthaiḥ  PNc 
prakṛtiḥ kila yasya te parītā pariṇāmena tadantare 'tra haṃsaḥ 
śayanāntagataṃ mṛṇālaśaṅki shṛtavān hāram adhīralocanāyāḥ  PNc 
SYNTAX sandānitakam
udaḍīyata khe mukhena bibhrad bhujagendrapratimaṃ tam añjasā sa

malyavatyā uttaram

bhramarīvāravindasya sudhāsahacaram madhu  PNc 
ānīyatākulatvaṃ sā tritīyena tanūdarī 
vismayenātisāndreṇa madena madanena ca  PNc

śaratprasanne saritaḥ pratimendur iva ambhasi  PNc 
stanapatralatāṃ tasyā bibheda pulakodgamaḥ 
satyaṃ yadantaraṅgeṇa bahiraṅgo nirasyate  PNc

rathāṅganāmamithune sāyantana ivānilaḥ  PNc

śaṅke śaram ṛjūkurvan dadṛśe manmathas tayā

gadgadākṣaram avyaktaṃ kṛcchrāt prativaco dadau  PNc 
citravartiny api nṛpe tattvāveśena cetasi 
vrīḍārdhavalitaṃ cakre mukhendum avaśaiva sā  PNc 
dṛṣṭā sakhībhiḥ sākūtaṃ sā bālādharapallave 
dadhau vailakṣyahasitaṃ prasūnam iva mādhavī  PNc 
navaṃ prema navotkaṇṭhā navās te te manorathāḥ 
iti tasyās tathaivābhūd antaraṅgaḥ paricchadaḥ  PNc 
kiṃcit trapānuviddhena puṇḍarīkadalatviṣā 
tam ānarceva rājendum animittasmitena sā  PNc 
sā ca doḥśayitabhuvā nṛpeṇāddhyāsitā hṛdi 
kṛtāṅgabhaṅgavalanā jhaṭity ālasyam āyayau  PNc 
tatkṣaṇenaiva sā citraṃ tanvī tanmayatāṃ yayau 
kaṃ na pratārayaty eṣa kitavaḥ kusumāyudhaḥ  PNc 
stimitevāvatasthe sā sāraṅgāyatalocanā 
acetaneva śūnyeva suptevālikhiteva ca  PNc 
smareṇa marmaṇi kvāpi sāvidhyata sumadhyamā 
anidritāpi yat sābhūt kṣaṇaṃ mukulitekṣaṇā  PNc 
vyañcitānaṅgalīlena śṛṅgārarasabandhunā 
tanvī navānurāgeṇa sānyaiva ghaṭitābhavat  PNc 
ṛjunā aikṣata yac citraṃ yad abhūc ca trapāvatī 
tenātigūḍhabhāvāpi sā sakhībhir alakṣyata  PNc 
athānaṅgavatī nāma sakhī tām ity avocata 
daśanajyotsnayāraṇyaṃ sudhayeva niṣiñcatī  PNc 
kac cid asya pramodāya kumudasyeva cakṣuṣaḥ 
ayaṃ madhyamalokenduḥ pātālendukale tava  PNc 
vanānilāhṛtonnidra padmakesaraśālinā 
romodgama ivānena dhṛtas tvadavalokanāt  PNc 
adya naḥ saphalaṃ cakṣuś citre yad avalokitaḥ 
kandarpādhikakānto 'yam avantimṛgalāñchanaḥ  PNc 
tvām apy avāñcitāṃ manye yat tvayaitasya vakṣasi 
ete savibhramaṃ nyaste dṛśau muktālate iva  PNc 
jitam etena ko 'py eṣa satyaṃ kāmo 'sya kiṅkaraḥ 
ārohati parāṃ koṭim atra yat tava sambhramaḥ  PNc 
tvam atra baddhabhāveva kim indumukhi lajjase 
vilaṅghayaty alaṅghyāni smaradurlalitāni kaḥ  PNc 
ko 'nyaḥ sakhi nṛśaṃso 'sti kāmaṃ viṣamabāṇataḥ 
sukumāre tavāpy aṅge yena vyāpāritaḥ śaraḥ  PNc 
bimbauṣṭhe eva rāgas te tanvi pūrvam adṛśyata 
adhunā hṛdaye 'py eṣa mṛgaśāvākṣi lakṣyate  PNc 
ekena rājahaṃsena hṛto hāras tanūdari 
anena tu dvitīyena likhitenāpi te manaḥ  PNc 
kutas trapā tavālīṣu kiṃcid unnamayānanam 
aho bata tvam etasminn atyāyatakutūhalā  PNc 
etat karṇotpalaṃ lolam apāṅgaprativeśitam 
tvad udantam ivaitasya kathayaty alikūjitaiḥ  PNc 
aho dūrasthitenāpi hṛdi spṛṣṭā nṛpendunā 
indukāntaśileva tvam ārdratām avagāhase  PNc 
nipuṇe niḥśvasiṣy evam atigūḍhaṃ yathā yathā 
tathā tathā tava vyaktam ayam ucchvasati smaraḥ  PNc 
smitam etad alolākṣi lajjāsaṃvalitaṃ tava 
idaṃ nirjitabālyasya yauvanasyoditaṃ yaśaḥ  PNc 
yathā taveyam aratir yathā sutanu vepase 
tathā kavacitaḥ śaṅke niḥśaṅkaṃ madanas tvayi  PNc 
kim atra karavai gāḍham ākalpakam idaṃ tava 
iyaṃ ca manmathasyāstraṃ nirgatā cūtamañjarī  PNc 
surataklāntaśabarī kabarīmālyacumbinaḥ 
katham ete tvayā tanvi sahyā malayavāyavaḥ  PNc 
kiṃ tāmyasi tavopāntam ānayāmy adhunaiva tam 
ity āśvāsayatīva tvām kokilo 'yaṃ kalasvanaḥ  PNc 
kūjantī kokilavadhūr iyam ādhiṃ dhunoti te 
anaṅganṛpasāmrājya līlāmaṅgalagāyinī  PNc 
vanāntadevatāvāpta pādanyāsotsavaḥ sphuṭam 
eṣa stabakito 'śokaḥ suhṛt kāmasya kā gatiḥ  PNc 
atrorvītilake dṛṣṭim asyantīṃ tilakaḥ krudhā 
ayaṃ tarjayatīva tvāṃ vātādhūtalatāṅguliḥ  PNc 
pathi smarasya viṣame skhalitāyām itas tvayi 
smitacchaṭeva niryāti sinduvārasya mañjarī  PNc 
drāghayaty astabimbauṣṭha ruciniḥśvasitāni te 
ayaṃ mukulitaḥ kiṃcid bakulo mukulastani  PNc 
latayā karṇikārasya puraḥ puṣpitayānayā 
anaṅgasyaikarājye 'smin hemavetralatāyitam  PNc 
aho na kasya bhindanti hṛdayaṃ vīkṣitā api 
nisargamṛdavo 'py ete sahakāranavāṅkurāḥ  PNc 
caturāṃ kokilām eṣa kṛtvā kurabako mukhe 
durlabhaṃ yācatīva tvāṃ līlāliṅganadohadam  PNc 
aśokaskandhalagneyaṃ kusumair navamādhavī 
prārthanīyapriyasparśāṃ hasati tvām ivotsukām  PNc 
bhūpatāv anuraktāyās tava santāpadīpanam 
sthalāravindaṃ serṣyeva sūte sakhi vasundharā  PNc 
amīṣv aṅkasthakandarpa jagadvijagayasiddhiṣu 
dṛṣṭir udvijate tanvi pāṭalākuḍmaleṣu te  PNc 
sundari dvitayasyātra kraśimā bhūṣaṇāyate 
rājanyābaddhabhāvāyās tava rātreś ca samprati  PNc 
eṣa caitrotsavaś citre nṛpo 'yaṃ nūtanaṃ vayaḥ 
prāptāvakāśaḥ kāmo 'pi patitāsyatisaṅkaṭe  PNc 
kim ālikhitavaty eṣā citre mālyavatī nṛpam 
dvārīkṛteyam athavā vāmena vidhinā tava  PNc 
bahunā kiṃ cakorākṣi chalitāsi manobhuvā

ityādi vyāharantī sā kṛtabhrūbhaṅgayā tayā 
narendrabāṇapuṅkhena kuce kiṃ cid atudyata  PNc 
kalāvatīvacanam
atha kinnararājendra kanyā nāmnā kalāvatī 
evaṃ vacaḥ smitasudhā niṣiktākṣaram ādade  PNc 
kāmaṃ durlabham evaitac caitraś candrāṅkitā niśāḥ 
preyān vipañcīraṇitaṃ pañcabāṇāṅkitaṃ vayaḥ  PNc 
ayi tvāṃ mlāpayaty eṣa kālaḥ kamalalocane 
jagadāhlādajanakaḥ sudhāsūtir ivābjinīm  PNc 
sthāne tavānurāgo 'yam anaṅgasyāyam utsavaḥ 
sakhi snihyati nirvyājam indāv eva kumudvatī  PNc 
nṛpasyāraṇyasañcāraḥ śareṇānena sūcyate 
marutā dviradasyeva madaniṣyandagandhinā  PNc 
avaśyaṃ tanvi cinvānā vane haṃsam itas tataḥ 
kvacid vilokayiṣyanti taṃ tvatparijanastriyaḥ  PNc 
jñātatvadiṅgitaivātra taṃ ced drakṣyati pāṭalā 
tato 'sya ṣaṭpadasyeva balāc ceto hariṣyati  PNc 
sthirā bhava nṛpena tvam iha saṃyogam āpsyasi 
yathā kaṇvāśrame pūrvaṃ duṣyantena śakuntalā  PNc 
iti tadvacasaḥ sīmni masṛṇotkampitastanī 
vyājasācīkṛtamukhaṃ niśaśvāsa śaśiprabhā  PNc 
vanaśrīratnamañjīro latākuñjodare tataḥ 
cukūja mañjukaṇṭhas tāṃ dakṣiṇena kapiñjalaḥ  PNc 
harṣāśrulavakīrṇena satpatrāvalicāruṇā 
vāmena pasphure tasyāś cakṣuṣā ca stanena ca  PNc 
atrāntare samāyāntī dadṛśe dūratas tayā 
narendrasavitus tasya puraḥ sandhyeva pāṭalā  PNc 
tasyās traye ca tritayam apaśyat phaṇikanyakā 
mukhe smitaṃ kare hāraṃ sitam aṃse ca cāmaram  PNc 
sā hārahastā ruruce dhṛtastimitacāmarā 
sarasī suptahaṃseva phenādhyāsitapaṅkajā  PNc 
dṛṣṭiḥ phanīndraduhitur atikramyaiva pāṭalām 
bhṛṅgaśreṇir ivāśoke papātāvantibhartari  PNc 
priyaṃ naḥ sa ayam āyāti paśya paśya śaśiprabhe 
paramārānvayodāra hāramadhyamaṇir nṛpas  PNc 
iti priyasakhīsūkti sudhāniṣyandalekhayā 
sikte tadābhavat tasyāḥ smaraḥ pallavito hṛdi  PNc 
SYNTAX sandānitakam
sudhārasa ivorvībhṛt tayā saṃmukham āpatan 
dṛśā sphaṭikaśuktyeva vāraṃvāram apīyata  PNc 
vitene 'py ahikanyābhiḥ kautukenātanīyasā 
tasyāgre rājahaṃsasya netrendīvaravāgurā  PNc 
avantitilakodantam upasṛtyātha pāṭalā 
anaṅgadīpanaṃ tasyai jagādeṅgitavedinī  PNc 
deva paścātsthito 'py agre prāptaḥ paryutsuko bhavān 
ity abhāṣyata bhūpālaḥ citre caturayā tayā  PNc 
abhūt paryākulā sā ca muhūrtam asitekṣaṇā 
paścād alajjatālībhis tathā sasmitam īkṣitā  PNc 
tasyai hāraṃ mahībhartur arpayām āsa pāṭalā 
ākṛṣya bhartum ānītam atiśuddham iva āśayam  PNc 
sakhīnām anurodhena sā kilānaṅgamohitā 
hṛdi dīrghaguṇaṃ dadhre hāraṃ priyam ivāparam  PNc 
tuṣārapāṇḍunā tena vavṛdhe 'syā manobhavaḥ 
digantavāntajyotsnena mahodadhir ivendunā  PNc 
puṣpodgameneva latā prasādeneva bhāratī 
sā tena reje hāreṇa yaśaseva narendratā  PNc 
tataḥ śithilaparyasta vilolakabarīlatā 
ketuyaṣṭir iva śyāma patākāṅgā hiraṇmayī  PNc 
vasaṃtakamalollāsi mattabhramaraniḥsvanā 
dīpamānopadeśeva svarahasye manobhuvaḥ  PNc 
ullasatkuṭajācchāccha vilāsahasitacchaviḥ 
jhaṭity uadadhiveleva nirgacchad amṛtacchaṭā  PNc 
sarojinīva haṃsībhir bhṛṅgībhir iva mālatī 
śaśilekheva tārābhiḥ sakhībhir abhito vṛtā  PNc 
dṛṣṭvā narandram āyāntam udasthād utsukātha sā 
dadhatī nūtanaprema pariṇītām adhīratām  PNc 
SYNTAX kulakam
atha sutanur alolatārake sā suciram udañcitadīrghapakṣmamāle 
śaśina iva navodgatasya dūrāt avanipateḥ pathi locane mumoca  PNc 
āsannānucaradhṛtena paṅkajinyāḥ patreṇa sphuṭaghaṭitātapatralīlaḥ 
saś cchāyām atha mahasā hasan himāṃśoḥ kṣmāpālaḥ pulinam avāpa narmadāyās  PNc 
 iti śrīmṛgāṅkaguptasūnoḥ parimalāparanāmnaḥ padmaguptasya kṛtau navasāhasāṅkacarite mahākāvye śaśiprabhādarśano nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ  
saptamaḥ sargaḥ
śaśiprabhādarśanam
tataḥ sa dūrād ahirājakanyakāṃ javaikamitreṇā yutāṃ patatriṇā 
viśāmpatidīrghaguṇānuṣaṅgiṇīm anaṅgakodaṇḍalatām ivaikṣata  PNc 
upoḍhalāvaṇyataraṅgabhaṅgayā sarāgabimbauṣṭhagalatpravālayā 
ahāri lolaṃ nṛpates tayā balāt anaṅgaratnākaravelayā manaḥ  PNc 
ramāṅgadakṛtaṃ śaśiprabhāvarṇanam
savismayo locanamārgam āptayā tayā saḥ pātālatalendulekhayā 
athettham amlānamanorathodgamo ramāṅgadenābhidadhe narādhipaḥ  PNc 
avaimi saiveyam amogham āyudhaṃ manobhuvaḥ pannagarājakanyakā 
udaṃśulekhena mukhena kurvatī jagad vilīnenduvilokanaspṛham  PNc 
narendra satyaṃ saḥ kutūhalī bhaved alaukikaṃ rūpam avekṣituṃ rateḥ 
iyaṃ na yasyātithitāṃ gatā dṛśor agādhalāvaṇyasarit sumadhyamā  PNc 
iyaṃ sudhā mugdhavilāsajanmabhūr iyaṃ bhujaṅgālayaratnadīpikā 
iyaṃ jagannetracakoracandrikā puraḥ patākeyam ayugmapatriṇaḥ  PNc 
iyattayā muktam avaimi naipuṇaṃ prajāpater adbhutaśilpakarmaṇi 
nṛpopamānām upamānatāṃ gataṃ vinirmitaṃ yena hi ratnam īdṛśam  PNc 
iyaṃ tavānena virājatetarāṃ karasthitenāvanipālapatriṇā 
upeyuṣā kāñcanapadmam aṃśunā himetarāṃśor iva jahnukanyakā  PNc 
arālakeśīyam anena bhāti te śareṇa kārtasvarapuṅkhaśobhinā 
nisargagaureṇa narendraraśminā sakajjalā dīpaśikheva śārvarī  PNc 
iyaṃ vilāsorminimagnaśaiśavaṃ svibhāvyamānastanakuḍmalodgamam 
madaikavisrambhagṛhaṃ vigāhate vayo vibhaktāṅgam anaṅgadohadam  PNc 
iyaṃ natāṅgī jagadekasundare nideśite pāṭalayā nṛpa tvayi 
dṛśau navendīvarapatrapeśale vimuñcati śrīr iva śārṅgadhanvani  PNc 
anaṅgasāmrājyavilāsacāmare vanānilavyākulite 'ṃsucumbini 
pariślathe saṃyamanārtham etayā salīlam astaḥ kabarībhare karaḥ  PNc 
vilokayantī kusumaṃ kacāgrataś cyutaṃ kucasparśadhiyeva vakṣasi 
iyaṃ kṛśāṅgī kusumāstraśaṅkayā kṛtapraṇāmeva tavāvalokyate  PNc 
vilokayāsyāḥ kṣitipāla bibhratīṃ pradīpaśobhāṃ kabarīṃ niśāmukhe 
amī muhuḥ kuṅkumakesarāruṇā lasanti sīmantamaṇer marīcayaḥ  PNc 
virājate 'syās tilako 'yam añcito vikuñcitabhrūlatikāntare nṛpa 
vijitya lokadvitayaṃ divaṃ prati smareṇa bāṇo dhanuṣīva saṃhitaḥ  PNc 
apāṅgasaṃvardhitaśoṇakāntinā sukṛṣṇatāreṇa tuṣārapāṇḍunā 
iyaṃ pravālāsitaratnamauktikair vinirmiteneva cakāsti cakṣuṣā  PNc 
iyaṃ puro niryatidūram āyate kapolataḥ kāñcanakuṇḍalārciṣi 
iṣuṃ ruṣeva pratibhoktum udyatā manobhuve muktaśilīmukhe hṛdi  PNc 
iyaṃ triyāmāpatikāntipeśalaṃ vibuddhabandhūkadalādhikatviṣā 
bibharti bimbādharamudrayā mukhaṃ manobhirāmaṃ rajanīva sandhyayā  PNc 
upoḍhatārāpatitārahārayor iyaṃ yugena stanayor virājate 
dvayena deva uṣasi cakravākayoḥ saridgṛhītaikamṛṇālayor iva  PNc 
surāpagāvīcivipāṇḍur eṣa te cireṇa hāraś caritārthatāṃ gataḥ 
dhṛtaḥ kṣitīśa praṇayārdrayānayā salīlam utkampini yat kucadvaye  PNc 
iyaṃ mahīpāla vilokitena te vigāhate kāntam idaṃ daśāntaram 
bhavaty anārūḍhavikāsavibhramā kim udgame candramasaḥ kumudvatī  PNc 
kim anyad uktaṃ sudhayeva sāndrayā tad anyathā nātha na pāṭalavacaḥ 
sphuṭeyam asyāḥ kurute yad aṅgake balāt pariṣvaṅgam anaṅgavikriyā  PNc 
śaśiprabhāsamīpagamanam
itīṅgitajñe vadati priyaṃvade ramāṅgadena smitam udgatasmitaḥ 
avāpa paryāptaśaśāṅkadarśanaḥ phanīndrakanyāsavidhaṃ narādhipaḥ  PNc 
nāyikāceṣṭāḥ
uvāha lajjānatam añcitālakaṃ tato bhujaṅgādhipateḥ sutāmukhaṃ 
avāñcitaṃ kiṃ cana mātariśvanā saṣaṭpadaṃ padmam ivāravindinī  PNc 
pataty adhaḥ kuṅkumapaṅkapāṭale mayūkhalekhāpaṭale śikhāmaṇeḥ 
hriyeva raktāṃśukapallavas tayā pidhātum ālekhyanṛpe nyadhīyata  PNc 
nṛpasya citre madhureyam ākṛtir na bhidyate candramaso yathāmbhasi 
sakhījanas tām iti narmapeśalaḥ śanais trapānamramukhīm abhāṣata  PNc 
yathāsmi vaktāsi tathāsya bhūpater yadā punaḥ karṇasamīpam āpsyasi 
itīva nirvyājam udīrya tatyaje tayāyatākṣyā sa narendrasāyakaḥ  PNc 
alaṃ hriyaivaṃ samupekṣya gṛhyatām ayaṃ hi pāṇigrahaṇocitas tava 
itīrayantyāḥ kuṭilaṃ vacaḥ karād anaṅgavatyāḥ kamalaṃ jahāra sā  PNc 
atha svabimbādharapāṭalacchadaṃ kareṇa tattatsadṛśena bibhratī 
niṣevitum bhūpatim abhyupāgatā rameva rājīvamukhī rarāja sā  PNc 
dṛśas tatas tatparivārayoṣitāṃ netrāñjanaśyāmalapakṣmarājayaḥ 
śaśiprabhe bhūmipatau sakautukāḥ samāpatan kunda ivālipaṅktayaḥ  PNc 
nṛpārhaṇam
nipīyamānasya tayā śanaiḥśanair apāṅgasañcāritadīrghanetrayā 
upāttapuṣpaḥ kṣitibhartur arhaṇāṃ cakāra tasyāś caturaḥ sakhījanaḥ  PNc 
puraḥ śirasy āhitamanmathājñayā tayā kaṭākṣaiḥ kuṭajair ivārcitaḥ 
nṛpaḥ saparyāṃ punaruktasaṃvidāṃ sas tadvayasyānihitāv amanyata  PNc 
sarāgavaty utkalikābhir ākule mṛduny alaṃ pāṭalayā samarpite 
atha nyaṣīdannavapallavāsane phanīndrakanyāmanasīva pārthivaḥ  PNc 
anu kṣitīśaṃ nalinīdalāsane kayā cid āste parivārayoṣitā 
ramāṅgado 'py āsanabandham ādade vasundharāyāṃ vinayaikabandhuḥ  PNc 
śramānurodhād upaviśyatām itaḥ kṣaṇaṃ kṛśāṅgīti sakhībhir arthitā 
upāviśad vepitavāmanastanī tataḥ samaṃ tābhir ahīndrakanyakā  PNc 
nāyikāvilasitāni
vivartayantī vadanendumaṇḍalaṃ viśālanetrāntaniṣaktatārakam 
dvayena sā kṛṣyata sundarī samaṃ hriyā nṛpālokanakautukena ca  PNc 
athāvataṃsīkṛtalocanotpalaṃ kapoladolāyitaratnakuṇḍalam 
ciraṃ papau saḥ stimitena cakṣuṣā tadānanaṃ mālavamīnaketanaḥ  PNc 
kṛtī dṛśāsyāḥ sudṛśaḥ pibaty ayaṃ kapolalāvaṇyasudhāṃ narādhipaḥ 
mithaḥ sakhīnām iti sasmitaṃ vaco niśamya sābhūd adhikādhikatrapā  PNc 
manāg ivāṃsād apavartitānanā nirīkṣya taṃ bhūpatim arpitekṣaṇam 
vihasya lajjāmukule cakarṣa sā balād apāṅgaprasṛte vilocane  PNc

navasāhasāṅka
na tavāsurād ahaṃ kalayāmi samprati kim apy atādṛśam

vajrāṅkuśavākyam

dattābhayopanatapauraśatārpyamāṇa ratnopadhām atha sa ratnavatīṃ praviśya 
taṃ saṃyugasphuṭaparīkṣitaśauryasāraṃ rājye ripoḥ phaṇikumārakam abhyaṣiñcat  PNc 
mūrtaṃ manoratham ivopavanāt sakandam ādāya tat kanakakokanadaṃ narendraḥ 
ādātum īpsitamahīndrasuteti ratnam abhyutsukas tad anu bhogavatīṃ pratasthe  PNc 
devaḥ sāhasiko 'py amandamurajadhvānānumeyotsavām unnamraiḥ parito mahīṃ maṇigṛhair uttambhayantīm iva 
tām atyunnataratnatoraṇaśikhāpreṅkholamuktāphala prālambocchaladacchakāntinikarasmerām avāpat purīm  PNc 
 iti śrīmṛgāṅkadattasūnoḥ parimalāparanāmnaḥ padmaguptasya kṛtau navasāhasāṅkacarite mahākāvye hemakamalaharaṇo nāma saptadaśaḥ sargaḥ  
aṣṭādaśaḥ sargaḥ
phaṇirājadarśanam
taṃ viṣṭapatritayakaṇṭakadṛṣṭasāram abhyāgataṃ nṛpatim udgatagāḍhaharṣaḥ 
pratyudyayāv adhipatiḥ phaṇinām anargha ratnārghapāṇiraśanair atha śaṅkhapālaḥ  PNc 
purapraveśaḥ
ādāya sādaraphaṇīśvaradattam arghyam arghyaḥ satāṃ sa bahir eva niveśya sainyam 
devo 'viśad vinayavān puram agrayāyi vidyādharādhiparamāṅgadaratnacūḍaḥ  PNc 
utsṛjya gītam asamāpya vilāsalāsyam aṅkād apāsya sahasā maṇivallakīṃ ca 
atyunmanās tadavalokanakautukena vātāyanāny adhiruroha purandhrilokaḥ  PNc 
utkṣipya vepathumatā karapallavena vātāyanāgramaṇimauktikalājakāni 
smitvaikayā sa vilasan makarāvacūla līlālavāñcitavilocanam āluloke  PNc 
udyadvivṛttakaraveṇikayā nṛpendau tasmin smarollasitajṛmbhikayā kayā cit 
muktā muhur vibudhasindhukalindakanyā kirmīravārilaharīsuhṛdaḥ kaṭākṣāḥ  PNc 
vācālaratnavalayā savilāsam asmin nikṣipya kāpi navamauktikalājamuṣṭim 
tattāḍitāṃsataṭapārthivadattadṛṣṭir dīrghekṣaṇā kim iva na trapayā cakāra  PNc 
vakṣo dadhānam amarādriśilāviśālam ājānubāhum avalokya narendracandram 
cittopanītaparirambhasukhātisāndram anyā payodharabhare pulakaṃ babhāra  PNc 
ālokya darpaṇatale pratimāgataṃ tam ātto mayaiṣa' iti kāpi kṛtotsavābhūt 
mugdhā gate 'tha purato 'tra tadīyabimbe śūnyātmadarśavidhurendumukhī babhūva  PNc 
ity āpatan madanabāṇaparamparāṇām unmīlitāṅgavalanaślathamekhalānām 
eṇīdṛśāṃ vicarati sma sa rājahaṃsaḥ pārollasannavarasormiṣu mānaseṣu  PNc 
nāyakavarṇanam
saṅgītaveśmani phaṇīśvaracāraṇānāṃ gīteṣv ajasram iha śuśruma yad yaśāṃsi 
yātaḥ sa eva nayanātithitām ayaṃ naḥ puṇyair aho bata nṛpo navasāhasāṅkaḥ  PNc 
kāntichaṭāchuritadiktaṭa eṣa devo jīyājjaganti paramārakulapradīpaḥ 
unmūlya saṃprati surāritamaḥ samūlaṃ yenāhiviṣṭapatale vihitaḥ prakāśaḥ  PNc 
hantaiṣa pannagapater atulapratijñā prāgbhārasāgarasamuttaraṇaikapotaḥ 
utpākam eṣa ca phalaṃ phaṇirājakanyā citte ciraṃ kṛtapadasya manorathasya  PNc 
etad yaśobhaṭakare kanakāmbujaṃ tal līlāvataṃsam acirād viracayya yena 
pratyuptakalpatarupallavam eṣa pāṇim ādāsyate nṛpatir adya śaśiprabhāyāḥ  PNc 
hāṭakeśvaradarśanam
sāndrānurāgapiśunāḥ paraśuḥ pareṣām ākarṇayann iti saḥ paurajanasya vācaḥ 
śrīhāṭakeśvara iti prathitasya tuṅgam agre dadarśa maṇimandiram indumauleḥ  PNc 
SYNTAX kulakam
tatra praviśya sakṛtānatir ādidevam ānarca kalpaviṭapiprabhavaiḥ prasūnaiḥ 
stotuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ kuṭajāvadāta dantāṃśupallavitavāg upacakrame ca  PNc 
hāṭakeśvarastutiḥ
antarjatāpihitasomasurāpagāya pracchannaśaraśāsanalocanāya 
tīvravrataglapitaśailasutāsvarūpa vijñānanarmapaṭave baṭave namas te  PNc 
atyādarānatasurāsuramauliratna nānāmarīcikhacitāṅghrisaroruhāya 
dehārdhavartigirijāvihitābhyasūya sandhyāpraṇāmaviṣamāñjalaye namas te  PNc 
nīrandhrasindhujalasiktakapālamukta ratnāṅkurasya karaṇīṃ vidhurātanoti 
maulau sadaiva bhavato bhavabhedakartur nirdagdhabhāskaramahāya namo 'stu tasmai  PNc 
kandarpadarpaśamanāya kṛtāntahartre kartre śubhasya bhujagādhipaveṣṭanāya 
urvīmarudraviniśākaravahnitoya yājyāmbaroccavapuṣe supuṣe namas te  PNc 
nīrandhrabhūtidhavalāya gajendrakṛtti saṃvītadehakavalīkṛtapannagāya 
nirdagdhadānavakulāya vipatkṣayaika kāryāya kāraṇanutāya namo 'stu tubhyam  PNc 
te te yam eva kila vāṅmayasāgarasya pāraṃ gatāḥ praṇavam ātmavido vadanti 
tasmai samāhitamaharṣivinidrahṛdya hṛtpuṇḍarīkavihitasthitaye namas te  PNc 
uttaṃsitenduśakalāya kapālajūṭa saṅghaṭṭitormimukharāmbaranirjharāya 
bhasmāṅgarāgaśucaye vikacopavīta vyālendumaulimaṇidīdhitaye namas te  PNc 
nāstraṃ na bhasma na jaṭā na kapāladāma nenduḥ siddhataṭinī na phaṇīndrahāraḥ 
nokṣā viṣaṃ na dayitāpi na yatra rūpam avyaktam īśa kila tad dadhate namas te  PNc 
nāgarājagamanam
stutvety avantipatir indukulāvataṃsaṃ tanmandirāt sahacaraiḥ saha nirjagāma 
antarniveśitaharinmaṇivedi valgan nāgāṅganaṃ saḥ phaṇirājagṛhaṃ jagāma  PNc 
tatrāvatīrya rathataḥ sa ramāṅgadātta pāṇiḥ samucchalitamaṅgalatūryaghoṣe 
unnidrasāndrakusumaprakarāvakīrṇa māṇikyakuṭṭimatale masṛṇam viveśa  PNc

tatkṛtaḥ satkāraḥ
tasmin gate nayanagocaram uddhṛtārau baddhāñjalir jhaṭiti pannagarājasaṃsat

nyañcacchikhābharaṇabhāsurapadmarāga rocichaṭāghaṭitatatphaṇaratnakāntiḥ 
rājanyamaulimaṇicumbitapādapīṭhas tasmai cakāra sa mahābhijanaḥ praṇāmam  PNc 
pratyuptaratnam abhitaḥ pramadāvakīrṇaṃ muktvā catuṣkam uragendranideśitaṃ sa 
adhyāsta sādarajaratphaṇikalpitāśīs tanmadhyavartikanakāsanam unnatāṃsaḥ  PNc 
vatsāṃ vrajanāya mameti śanair visṛjya nepathyanīlamaṇiveśmani ratnacūḍam 
tatrāsanadvayam adāpayad asya pārśve vidyādharādhipayaśobhaṭayoḥ phaṇīndraḥ  PNc 
svarṇāsane svayam athācchaphaṇātapatra ratnapradīpaśatajarjaritāndhakāraḥ

citre niveśita ivātha yaśobhaṭena smitvā savismayam asūcyata pārthivāya  PNc 
śaśiprabhādarśanam
atrāntare pramadaloladṛśā nṛpeṇa dūrād adarśi phaṇirājasutābhiyāntī 
tanvī śirīśasumanaḥsukumāramūrtir devasya kārmukalateva manobhavasya  PNc 
jyotsnāsitāmbararucisnapitānanendur mātrācirodgatayavāṅkurakarṇapūram 
muktvojjvalaṃ lalitakautukakaṅkaṇaṃ ca veṣaṃ vivāhasamayocitam udvahantī  PNc

mālyavatīvākyam

vilambase kim

kamalāvataṃsaḥ
ukte tayety akṛta kāñcanapuṣkaraṃ tad yāvat saḥ karṇaśikhare phaṇirājaputryāḥ 
tāvad vihāya mṛgarūpam udāramūrtir agre babhūva puruṣo 'sya sahemavetraḥ  PNc 
puruṣaṃ prati praśnaḥ

pratīhārasya vṛttāntaḥ
kailāsaśailavasater giriśoparodhād dvārapraveśaviniṣedhakaṣāyitena

svaṃ rūpam āpsyasi tadeti samādideśa śāpāntam eṣa vihitānunayo maharṣiḥ  PNc

vivāhavidhiḥ
tūryasvaneṣu vilasatsu paṭhatsv amandaṃ bandiṣv anīyata phaṇīndrapurodhasā ca 
koṇāvasaktajalapūritaratnakumbhāṃ vediṃ tayā saha sa madhyamalokapālaḥ  PNc

phaṇipativākyam
nirgacchadaccharucinirbharam aṃśukena saṃchāditaṃ kim api pāṇitale dadhānaḥ 
ūce tam ity adhipatiḥ phaṇinām udañcat dantāṃśuśāritaradachadaratnakāntiḥ  PNc 
yad dīyate tava na tādṛśam asti kiṃcid gehe mamātra nṛpate navasāhasāṅka

śivaliṅgārpaṇam

svanagarīṃ prati prasthāpanam

ujjayinīpraveśaḥ
bālātapachuritaharmyaviṭaṅkavarti pārāvatātimadhuradhvanitachalena

mahākāleśvaradarśanam

śivaliṅgapratiṣṭhā

anuyāyiprasthānam

śaśiprabhāsakhīgamanam

sāmrājyalakṣmīsvīkāraḥ
nīlachatrāvataṃsā bhujagapatisutāpāṇḍugaṇḍasthalāntaḥ kastūrīpaṅkapatravyatikaraśabalavyāyatāṃse salīlam

atha granthapraśastiḥ
śrīmatkavipriyasuhṛcchaladaṅkarāma rājendubhaktyadhigatapratibhāviśeṣaḥ 
etad vinidrakusumadadyuti padmaguptaḥ śrīsindhurājanṛpateś caritaṃ babandha  PNcGp

nyastāni yāni mayi sūktisudhāpṛṣanti devena tena kati cit kavibāndhavena 
candrātapasnapitamauktikasodarāṇāṃ teṣām idaṃ vilasitaṃ navasāhasāṅka  PNcGp 
yac cāpalaṃ kim api mandhadhiyā mayaivam āsūtritaṃ narapate navasāhasāṅka
